# Full List of MariaDB Options, System and Status Variables

Alphabetical list of all [mariadbd Options](/kb/en/mariadbd-options-full-list/), [Server System Variables](../../server-usage/replication-cluster-multi-master/optimization-and-tuning/system-variables/server-system-variables.md) and [Server Status Variables](../../server-usage/replication-cluster-multi-master/optimization-and-tuning/system-variables/server-status-variables.md). The convention used is that variable names are listed with '_' and options with '-'.
